German Forces on the Western Front Appear to Be Taking the Offensive; Intense Artillery Battles Along the Entire Line Between the Moselle and Rhine Rivers 32

Rumor that Hitler Will Go to the Western Front to Command

Paris – The actions of German forces on the Western Front seem to be gradually taking on an offensive posture. The German army is heavily concentrated in the area between the Moselle and Saarbrücken, as the commander-in-chief is quite uneasy about the continuing pressure from the French forces there. The Germans have repeatedly launched attacks in this area, attempting to capture French soldiers for intelligence, but no French soldiers have been captured, as all German advances have been stopped by French machine guns. It is believed that Hitler's goal is to drive the French forces out of German territory. Intense artillery battles are taking place along the entire line between the Moselle and Rhine rivers, indicating that the German army will soon make a major effort to retake the Saarbrücken. However, the French forces are in a good defensive position, and the obstacles faced by the German army are extremely formidable. Therefore, any attempt by the German army to retake Saarbrücken will meet with serious resistance. To maintain its offensive, the German army will inevitably have to use 500,000 to 1,000,000 troops, and the extent of its losses will be astonishing. If the Germans choose a more accessible route, invading Verdun via Luxembourg, the French commander has already made preparations. It is believed that the Germans have another option, which is to launch an attack parallel to the Luxembourg border, flanking the Maginot Line on the Swiss side. The current concentration of German forces in the northern and southern parts of Germany suggests the possibility of adopting this strategy. (Reuters, 10th)

Paris – According to neutral sources, Hitler may arrive at the Western Front this week to assume the position of supreme commander of the German army. After that, Aviation Minister Göring will replace Hitler in taking actual command. His rank will be above the commander-in-chief of the German army, von Brauchitsch. At that time, Hitler's own lightning war plan will be adopted, replacing the strategy prepared by the General Staff over the years, which has progressed simultaneously with the Franco-German defense system. According to French war reports, enemy reconnaissance patrols were very active yesterday between the Moselle and Saar rivers on the Western Front. The enemy launched several attacks in this area, some of which were quite effective, but all were repelled by French forces. (Reuters, 11th)

Brussels – A Havas correspondent recently inspected the Belgian border and is deeply aware that the Belgian General Staff has taken effective military measures on the northern and eastern borders. King Leopold III has ordered that the details of border defenses not be disclosed, but it is generally believed that the border troops are well-trained, have high morale, are well-equipped, and have many flat-trajectory guns. Although Germany has stated that "if French forces invade Belgium, Germany is prepared to defend it," the people on the Belgian border generally believe that Germany has no intention of attacking the country, and they do not believe that French forces will invade the country. They also believe that if Germany launches a brazen attack on Belgium, they will do their best to resist. Furthermore, according to observers on the Belgian border, Germany has not concentrated heavy troops in the area near the Belgian border. However, from the city of Gemmenich to the border of the Grand Duchy of Luxembourg, there is an average of one soldier stationed every ten meters. In some places, artillery units and anti-aircraft units are also deployed. In addition, there are many trucks loaded with soldiers and military supplies heading to the Luxembourg border and the Siegfried Line in the German city of Malmedy. (Havas, 10th)

Paris – The General Headquarters has just issued War Bulletin No. 74, stating, "A large number of enemy patrols probed our military positions south of the cities of Saarlouis and Pirmasens last night and were repelled." Semi-official sources went on to explain that the goal of German activities in recent days has been to test the strength of our forward positions and the operational plans formulated by our General Staff, repeatedly attempting to capture our soldiers in order to obtain the truth, but without success. Yesterday, enemy patrols were present along the entire line (a total of 160 kilometers). These units, with ten men each, were tasked with reconnaissance of our positions. Some of them even approached our barbed wire defenses or crossed the barbed wire. At that time, both sides threw hand grenades at each other, and our army finally repelled them and inflicted heavy damage. (Havas, 11th)

Paris – The General Headquarters has just issued War Bulletin No. 71, stating, "Enemy patrol units were very active today between the Saar and Moselle rivers. There was an artillery battle between enemy and our forces between the Rhine and Moselle rivers. In addition, one of our warships attacked a German submarine, with considerable success." (Havas, 9th)

Paris – The General Headquarters has just issued War Bulletin No. 72, stating, "Enemy patrol units were active southeast of the Saar River yesterday. Artillery units on both sides also shelled each other in that area." (Havas, 10th)

Paris – The General Headquarters has just issued War Bulletin No. 73, stating, "Enemy troops were engaged in reconnaissance between the Saar and Moselle rivers today and launched repeated attacks, sometimes with considerable strength, but all were repelled by our side." (Havas, 10th)

Four British Planes Fly Reconnaissance Over Germany, Obtaining Important Photos 33

London – British journalist Clifford, who accompanied the British Air Force to France to observe the war, recently stated that four British planes conducted their first daytime reconnaissance flight over German territory along the German border from France to the North Sea. The headquarters received important information about (1) the evacuation of residents from several important German cities, (2) the concentration of German troops in Aachen, (3) the construction of fortresses on the Luxembourg border, and (4) the concentration of the German Air Force. Therefore, it sent planes directly into German territory to verify that this information was accurate. The results of the British reconnaissance are now being studied by experts. It is reported that the photos taken by two of the planes are extremely valuable. The four British planes were divided into two pairs and took off from a secret British airfield behind the Maginot Line. The first pair encountered bad weather, their altitude was often 6,000 feet, and they flew past the southernmost tip of Luxembourg, that is, the factory behind the French artillery shelling of the outer edge of the Siegfried Line, and continued to appear and disappear in the clouds to conduct reconnaissance of everything. When they reached Koblenz in German territory, German anti-aircraft gunners used the sound of the planes to determine the distance and direction of the British planes and fired. Shells passed through the clouds and exploded around the British planes, but the British planes were not hit and continued to advance. German gunners urgently notified other locations by telephone, so when the British planes flew to Siegburg, they were again subjected to heavy anti-aircraft fire, but they still passed safely and reached Aachen along the Belgian border. When they saw the Rhine River flowing west into the Netherlands, the weather became extremely bad, and they could not see anything looking down. Then they headed towards the German North Sea coast, carefully avoiding Dutch territory, and finally safely arrived at the designated British airfield. The first pair flew out before dawn, and when the sun rose on the mountains east of the Rhine River, they had been in German territory for a long time, and the weather was also suitable, so they were able to take the photos they obtained. (Reuters, 10th)

London – A Reuters war correspondent recently stated that the British Air Force on the Western Front is now preparing for its first real air battle with the enemy. All bombers and fighters have been distributed to secret airfields behind the battle line, waiting for orders to move out. British bombers have not yet shown their power on the Western Front, but they are gradually learning the skills of the German Air Force and anti-aircraft guns. (Reuters, 11th)

Amsterdam – According to travelers arriving here from Germany, a large number of anti-aircraft guns have now been stationed in the German territory along the German-Dutch border, fearing that the British Air Force will attack the Ruhr and other western industrial areas. (Reuters, 11th)

German Air Force Attacks British Fleet in the North Sea; Most of Five German Planes Land in Denmark 34

London – The Admiralty has just issued a bulletin, stating briefly, "One of our patrol ships discovered a German fleet in the sea southwest of Norway, and our fleet sailed to meet it, but because of the darkness, the enemy ships were able to escape. In addition, a team of German bombers attacked several of our cruisers and destroyers in the northeastern North Sea today. Our side immediately opened anti-aircraft guns to resist. As a result, our side suffered no damage, and the extent of the enemy's losses is also unclear." (Havas, 9th)

Danzig – News of the battle between several British cruisers and a team of German bombers in the North Sea last night has now been confirmed. It is estimated that there were two German planes which were forced to land in Danish territory. The third plane had heard it was landing in Norway territory, and the crew are being detained by the Norwegian government. There were also two German aircrafts in which one had fallen on the beach. The remaining plane flew above Jutland at very low altitudes. The Danish anti-aircraft fire was shooting it down. (Reuters, 10th)

London – Five German bombers engaged in combat with several British cruisers and destroyers in the North Sea yesterday. One of them crashed into the sea in Danish waters, another crashed into Sweden, and another flew low over Danish airspace while fleeing, and was fired on by the country's anti-aircraft guns. The other two, due to lack of gasoline, landed in Denmark. One was on Fanø Island, west of Esbjerg, and one pilot was injured and has been sent to the hospital. The others have been detained. The other was at Nymindegab harbor, north of Esbjerg, all four pilots are unharmed. They burned the plane themselves, claiming to Danish authorities that it was caused by a bomb explosion. They claimed they departed from south of Hamburg and flew for eight hours, dropping bombs on British warships and engaging in combat with British planes. Among these pilots, one was older and had participated in the Spanish Civil War and was wearing a medal presented by Spanish head of state General Franco. (Havas, 10th)

Copenhagen – A German military plane flew into Danish airspace near the port of Aabenraa in the southern German peninsula at 3:00 PM this afternoon. It was fired upon by anti-aircraft guns. The plane was reportedly forced to land near Nymindegab harbor in western Jutland at around 5:00 PM. The four pilots then burned the plane themselves and told the police that they were flying to the North Sea for reconnaissance and were forced to land in Denmark due to lack of gasoline. (Havas, 9th)

Berlin – An official statement this afternoon said that several German bombers flew to the vicinity of the west coast of Norway on the 9th of this month and attacked several British warships. Six of the bombs hit the vital points of the British cruisers, and the sound of the explosion was heard several miles away. Two German planes were forced to land in Danish waters. (Haitong, 10th)

Berlin – The official news agency announced today that German warships and planes had fought with British ships in the North Sea in the past few days. Some British ships were damaged, and the fighting is still ongoing. (Reuters, 11th)

British Warships Intercept Japanese Ships 35

Tokyo – Local newspapers are fiercely criticizing the British warships intercepting Japanese merchant ships, regarding it as a threat to Japanese interests. The Tokyo "Nichinichi Shimbun" stated that British ships have recently intercepted Japanese ships near Taiwan and Nagasaki. A British cruiser appeared near the Japanese coast at the end of September, a British warship was found between Japan and Taiwan in early October, and a British warship was found near the southern coast of Japan on October 7. These reports were all submitted by Japanese merchant ships. The newspapers said that the appearance of British ships near the Japanese coast has angered people in the Japanese shipping industry. The Japanese people find it difficult to understand the actions of these British ships. (Haitong, 11th)

Tokyo – British naval attaché Colonel Duffinell gave a statement today regarding the Japanese media reports that Japanese merchant ships had recently been intercepted by British ships near Japanese territorial waters. "Such actions may be surprising to the Japanese people, but they do not contain any meaning to deal with Japan. The British ships near Japanese territorial waters are only carrying out their routine patrol duties, as they do all over the world. This kind of action by British ships is normal in wartime. As for the interception of a few Japanese ships, it is only to determine whether they are indeed Japanese ships or German ships pretending to be. Therefore, the interception of Japanese ships by British ships should not be considered impolite to Japan and should not be viewed in that way. The British ships in the vicinity of Japanese territorial waters are entirely performing patrol duties in order to intercept German ships heading to or leaving Japan in the waters there." The Nichinichi Shimbun published a criticism of the Japanese reports that two Japanese ships had recently been intercepted by British ships near Wakayama and Nagasaki, saying that the Japanese side found the actions of the British authorities incomprehensible. " Reuters, 11th)

Neutral Country Ships: Two More Sinkings - Finnish Ship "India" Hits a Mine, Swedish Ship's Accident Cause Unknown 36

Amsterdam: According to local newspapers, the Finnish freighter "India," loaded with lumber, struck a mine on the 9th of this month within the British minefield six miles north of Terschelling. Two crew members were killed by the explosion, and the other twenty-odd people were rescued by the Swedish ship "Irisburg" and brought here. Four of them were injured, including two women. (Haitong Telegraph, 11th)

The Hague, Netherlands: The Finnish ship "India," with a tonnage of 2,070, struck a mine and sank this afternoon off the coast of Terschelling in the northern Netherlands. All crew members have been rescued. (Havas, 9th)

London: The Air Ministry has just issued a bulletin stating that the first group of war correspondents from British newspapers departed today for France to visit British Air Force bases. (Havas, 9th)

Stockholm, Sweden: The Swedish ship "Vistula," en route to Hull, England, sank suddenly today northeast of the Shetland Islands (in the Scottish Sea). The cause is unknown. Half of the eighteen crew members have been rescued. (Havas, 10th)

Brussels, Belgium: Regarding the repeated sinking of neutral country ships, the neutral governments will soon make representations to the German government. It is reported that the Belgian government will also participate. (Havas, 10th)

Stockholm: Fishing boats that passed through the Skagerrak Strait from the Baltic Sea into the North Sea issued a report today from Gothenburg, stating that they saw a large number of German armed fishing boats and small freighters heading north. They are likely intended to blockade Britain or serve as supply ships for German submarines in the North Sea and Atlantic Ocean. (Reuters, 10th)

London: The official list of the ninety-three missing passengers from the British ship "Athenia," torpedoed on September 4th, was formally released here tonight. It includes fifty British, thirty Americans, seven Poles, four Germans, and two stateless passengers. Combined with the previously reported nineteen missing crew members, the total number of casualties is one hundred and twelve. (Reuters, 9th)

London: First Lord of the Admiralty Winston Churchill stated this afternoon in the House of Commons that from August 24th to September 9th, British ships sunk by German submarines totaled 5,809 tons. During the same period, German ships sunk by British warships totaled 13,615 tons. In comparison, Germany's losses exceed ours by 7,806 tons. Furthermore, no British ships have been lost since September 9th. (Havas, 11th)

Japan Does Not Change Current Attitude; No Basis for Peace Negotiations 39

Quo Tai-chi's Speech

London: Chinese Ambassador to Britain Quo Tai-chi stated in a Double Tenth Day celebration speech today that as long as Japanese militarists hold power and do not change their current attitude, there can be no basis for negotiations or hope for peace. People throughout Europe and the world are now asking whether Europe can achieve a just and lasting peace. In my opinion, this answer is well known to us. Westerners can better understand the similar difficulties faced by China and Western democracies. Peace must be based on international good faith, international public law, human dignity, and respect for the principles of mutual life. (Reuters, 10th)

London: The Aid China Committee hosted a banquet in London today to celebrate the Double Tenth Day, the anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China. Lord Davies, Vice-Chairman of the League of Nations Union, presided, and there were a total of one hundred and fifty guests. Chinese Ambassador to Britain Quo Tai-chi delivered a speech. Lady Snowden, a director of the British Broadcasting Corporation, Ms. Fry, and former Labor Member of Parliament Sir Richard Stafford Cripps also delivered speeches. Chinese overseas gathered at the Chinese embassy this afternoon for a tea party and observed two minutes of silence to commemorate the soldiers and civilians who died in the war against Japan. They also telegraphed the Chinese army to wish them an early victory and an end to the war. (Reuters, 10th)

Turmoil Expands in Japanese Foreign Ministry; All Staff Resign; Personnel at Japanese Consulate General in Shanghai Also Resign 41

Tokyo: The government is now paying close attention to the disputes in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs caused by the establishment of the new Ministry of Trade. Therefore, on the 11th, the heads of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs were instructed to provide consideration if there are proposals within the scope of the Cabinet's decision. At the same time, senior members like Kenkichi Yoshizawa and Sueo Yamakawa were urged to mediate. As a result, the executive committee of the administrative authorities of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, starting from 12:30 PM, proposed and discussed a final compromise plan. However, after an all-staff meeting of section chiefs and administrative officials at 8:00 PM, the result of the discussion was a decision that all senior officials from section chief downwards would submit their resignations. Therefore, the decision-making official went to the Shibuya private residence at 9:00 PM the same afternoon to visit Foreign Minister Nomura to discuss the problem of handling the aftermath. As a result, it was decided to discuss everything regarding the response to the resignations at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs with the Foreign Minister on the morning of the 12th before determining the policies. (Domei, 11th)

Domei News Agency Shanghai: The unanimous resignation of the administrative authorities of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs in opposition to the establishment of the Ministry of Trade has affected foreign agencies. The Consulate General in Shanghai also held a meeting on the 11th to discuss how to deal with the issue within the ministry. As a result, Consul General Miura and fifteen senior officials, as well as twenty-six junior officials, decided to take the same attitude as all staff members of the ministry and immediately submitted their resignations. (11th)

Tokyo: Ministry of Foreign Affairs personnel held a meeting this morning to discuss changing from collective action to individual resignations. The committee organized by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs personnel had refused to accept the compromise offered by Foreign Minister Nomura yesterday afternoon, and the Foreign Minister also refused to submit the officials' plan to the Cabinet. Therefore, there was discussion of individual resignations. The "Nichinichi Shimbun" reported that the government will temporarily hold the resignations in abeyance and return them after the situation has eased. However, it will allow the departure of twenty-odd senior members who insist on a hard-line stance. (Reuters, 11th)

Guangdong Province Chinese Army Intensifies Mobilization for General Offensive on Guangzhou; Simultaneous Actions on Both Banks of the East River; Ammunition Depot of Japanese Army Attached to Shatin Explodes 42

Hong Kong Correspondence: The Chinese army is actively implementing a counter-offensive against Guangzhou. Zhang Fakui, acting commander of the ×th War Zone, has ordered the three armies of the east, west, and north, as well as the guerrillas, to intensify mobilization and cooperate with the central mechanized units to pressure Guangzhou. This decision for a counter-offensive has been prepared for a long time, and the training of guerrillas and the replenishment of regular army personnel have been satisfactorily resolved. It is said that the conscription is proceeding excellently. On the East River front, the overall offensive is being launched simultaneously from the Zengcong line on the north bank and the Dongbao line on the south bank. At the same time, efforts are being intensified to suppress bandits and traitors bought by ××× operating in Guishan and Elephant Head Mountain. The Liang Zhu unit of the Mou Detachment of the Third Column entered Elephant Head Mountain on the first of this month and captured many puppet "Revival Army" soldiers. Provincial guerrilla command chief Xiang Hanping has established a reformatory for puppet soldiers. If it is found that the puppet soldiers were acting under duress, they will all be taken in. The reformatory has only been open for a month, and the defection of puppet soldiers in Guangzhou is like a rising storm. Many puppet soldiers in the reformatory repent of being used by the Japanese. Therefore, when they hear that our army is counter-attacking Guangzhou, they are all willing to serve the country and act as guides. As a result, various traitors in Elephant Head Mountain flee at the first sign of trouble, and the bandits in Guishan have also ceased their activities. The military movements in Zengcong and Dongbao are recorded below.

Japanese Army Movements

The Guangzhou Japanese Army Headquarters is aware that the Chinese army is gradually launching a general counter-offensive. The Japanese army held a secret meeting to respond to the Chinese army. According to intelligence, the Japanese army authorities have ordered the Japanese army in Foshan and Sanshui to construct defensive works along the Guangzhou-Sanshui Road, adopting a defensive posture on the western front. The Japanese army is currently deploying troops in Central and Northwest China and cannot reinforce South China. However, they are extremely afraid that the Chinese army on the southern section of the Guangdong Road and the Zengcong line will attack Guangzhou directly. Therefore, there have been changes in the Japanese army's organization recently. A regiment is composed of a mixture of regular Japanese army, Taiwanese, Korean army, Northeast puppet army, and Guangdong puppet Revival Army. Japanese army tanks, armored vehicles, donkeys, and horses stationed in Guangzhou are being moved out one after another, and citizens are being forced to manufacture a large number of "Japanese flags" to create a deception and confuse the Chinese army. The ammunition and weapons stored in the Henan warehouse are being busily transported out.

Puppet Army Rebellion

The Guangzhou Japanese army has built many military depots in the Yantang and Shatin areas to store weapons and explosives. On the evening of the first of this month, the Shatin military depot suddenly exploded and caught fire. The commander of the Southern China Expeditionary Army, Ando Rikichi, suspected that it was caused by anti-war elements in the army. On the morning of the second, he sent a large force of military police to the eastern suburbs and arrested a total of 150 Korean soldiers, who were taken back to headquarters. The arrested Korean soldiers, because the war has been indefinite and they have been repeatedly attacked by our army and civilians, cannot sleep peacefully. The anti-war sentiment is growing stronger. It is said that this group of Korean soldiers will be sent back to Taiwan.

Fierce Battle in Zengcheng

On September 29th, the Japanese army sent twenty-two anti-tank guns and field guns from the Guangzhou-Huizhou Highway to Zengcheng. Japanese aircraft also scouted day and night in the areas around Zengcheng: Boluo, Zhengguo, Paitan, Luofu Mountain, Conghua, and Aotou. Traitors were sent to the villages near the war zone to threaten the public and attempt to seize food. A senior commander of the Mou Army Group of the Chinese army in Zengcheng recently inspected the positions on the front line and instructed Tan Sui, the commander of the Mou Army in charge of the Zengcong line, that the Chinese side's conscription and supply could be continuous. The elite new army of the Chinese side in Luofu Mountain has advanced towards Zengcheng. On September 30th, they arrived at the outer line of Zengcheng. They launched three attacks in the evening, and the new artillery remotely bombarded Zengcheng to cover the Chinese army's advance. The outposts exchanged fire for six hours that day. The Japanese army responded with mortars. The Japanese army in Zengcheng is now under pressure and looks as if they will retreat to the periphery of Zengcheng. The Chinese army in Zhengguo and Luofu Mountain is very excited. All units are advancing according to the original route to strengthen the front line. A major battle is about to begin.

Eastern Front Guerrillas: The Chinese army on the eastern front adopted a mobile warfare strategy, using the towering mountains of the East River as a base for annihilating the Japanese army. The puppet army of the Luofu Mountain Range has been completely suppressed by our Tan Sui's active suppression in September. This vast mountain range is specially used as a large base for deploying, training regular new troops and guerrillas. Recently, Guangdong Province received instructions from the Military Training Department and the Ministry of Military Affairs, unifying guerrilla education in Guangdong Province. The new guidelines have been issued to Guangdong, with Luofu Mountain and a certain two places as the guerrilla education zone. The Chen Shenrong unit of the Fourth Column was transferred for training. Because the Guangdong Provincial Guerrilla Team operates extensively, the method of mine collection and cycle training, the guerrilla warfare between Dongbao, is replaced by the security group of Chi Zhongkuan's unit and the guerrilla teams of Yuan Huazhao and Liu Fayu to engage in guerrilla warfare in the two counties in the east. Furthermore, the southern section of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway has been controlled by the Chinese army, and guerrilla positions have been established to inflict significant blows on the Japanese army at any time. Currently, the Guangzhou-Kowloon line is stationed from Buji and Pinghu to Shigutou, Lilang, Tiantangwei, Tangtouxia, and Zhangmutou, in large forces to deal with Japanese mechanized units. In order to cope with the Japanese mechanized unit operations, people everywhere were mobilized to participate enthusiastically in destroying the railway, dismantling the rails, and moving the sleepers elsewhere. The Japanese army in Shenzhen is also afraid of the Chinese army attacking along the railway, and after destroying the railway, they have added obstacles such as bamboo fences and barbed wire. Even if the Japanese army makes every effort to clear the Guangzhou-Kowloon Road after this contest, it will not be able to repair and open the road in a short period of time.

Japanese Army Captured

Recently, the Panyu militia has been attacking the Japanese army and carrying out sabotage in the Ping Mountain, Pingzhou, Weiyong, Lezhu, and Bijiang areas bordering Shunde, Nanhai, and Panyu. Although the Japanese army has repeatedly coordinated with the puppet pacification army to carry out so-called sweeps, they have gained nothing. The Chinese militia avoids the strong and attacks the weak. When the Japanese army arrives, it disintegrates into smaller units and disperses into the suburbs, making it impossible for the Japanese army to grasp. At 7:00 AM on the morning of the 28th of last month, Second Lieutenant Kawamoto Kunio (from Tokushima, Shikoku, Japan), a platoon leader of the 43rd Regiment of the 11th Division of the Japanese Army, drove a motorboat from Pingzhou to Guangzhou. The boat carried five Japanese soldiers and more than ten puppet soldiers. It arrived in Guangzhou at about 9:00 AM. At 10:00 AM, it returned from Guangzhou to Pingzhou. The boat was fully loaded with grain. When the boat sailed to the Ping Mountain waters on the border of Panyu and Nanhai, it was discovered by the He Wencan unit of the Chinese militia, who opened fire with machine guns and densely swept at it. First, the helmsman was killed. Because the boat had no one to drive it and the machinery was damaged, it ran aground on the sand and could not move. The Japanese and puppet armies exchanged fire with the militia for half an hour. Ammunition was exhausted and no reinforcements arrived. More than ten people were killed or injured. The rest jumped into the water and escaped. Kawamoto Kunio was captured alive by the militia because he was injured in the head and hands. Several Japanese rifles and a large quantity of grain were seized. On the 30th, he was escorted back to the Panyu County government and interrogated by Li Shuzong, the deputy commander of the Mou Guerrilla Zone and concurrently the magistrate of Panyu County. According to Kawamoto, he had recently been incorporated into the Fujita Transport Team and was transporting grain to Pingzhou that day.

Double Tenth Festival Football Match: Donghua Defeats St. Francis 2-1; Poor Ball Luck in First Half, Saving a Penalty Kick Reverses the Situation 44

On the Double Tenth Festival, Donghua played a friendly match against St. Francis at Yiyuan. As a result of Donghua's fierce attack, they only won by two to one. They were actually behind by zero to one in the first half. St. Francis' ball luck was particularly good, and Donghua's attacks repeatedly failed to score. Cabotto's goalkeeping was exceptional. In the middle of the second half, Donghua was penalized with another penalty kick. The misfortune in ball luck was consistent. However, Gu Biao blocked it successfully in a tense atmosphere. From then on, Donghua turned from bad luck to good, entering a smooth path, scoring two goals in a row and reversing the defeat into victory. Three thousand spectators cheered and shouted in a tense atmosphere. Donghua finally announced victory. Donghua attacked first,

Frequent Loss of Opportunities

Donghua attacked first for a long time but did not make any progress. Therefore, the second team rose up and made every effort to launch an attack. Unfortunately, fate was unkind, and all their efforts were in vain. A Dai's low shot hit the goal post and bounced out without any response, which was a pity. Jia Youliang repeatedly attacked the goal, but all were bounced out by the crossbar. After that, Donghua had an excellent opportunity to attack the goal, but none of the results were fruitful. Looking back at the St. Francis team, they were closely monitored by Donghua players. However, when it was 31 minutes into the game, Fuen raised the flag and launched a single-handed attack, passing to Kai Xu'erzi, who shot diagonally, taking the lead with one to zero. Donghua lost this city, and launched a major counterattack, still trapped in the unfortunate game of fate, and failed for a long time. The first half ended, Donghua was behind by zero to one,

Final Victory

After the lemon, Donghua's lineup was slightly changed. Chen Hongguang returned to the defense to protect the home. A Rong was transferred to the center back to adopt a three-inside-guard strategy. However, the momentum did not improve in the first ten minutes. Youliang's header did not go in, and A Dai's shot was caught again. At 15 minutes, Hongguang went deep into the penalty area and was penalized with a penalty kick. Fuen took the penalty, and Gu Biao jumped up and saved it. Therefore, the army counterattacked, and Cai Shengsen tied the score to one each in the crowd, winning a lot of applause. At 30 minutes, A Dai scored a low shot from 15 yards, establishing a 2-1 victory. Since then, Donghua's offensive has been strong. The overall result was 2-1. Donghua came from behind,

Inter-Port Football: Another Problem; Difficult to Achieve at Christmas, Further Discussion Needed Next Spring 45

(Hong Kong News) The Hong Kong Football Association held a monthly meeting at 5:30 pm on the second day, in the conference room on the fifth floor of the Guangdong Bank. Attendees included Bi Lite (Hong Kong Club), Fen Dang (Kowloon Club), Chen Hanming (South China Club), Ju Bi (Police), Jian Jin (St. Joseph's), Li Huitang (Association), Wen Wu (Midushixi), Bin Wu (Army), and Gu Ba (Navy). The agenda started at 5:40 pm and lasted one hour. First, the routine cases of the previous month were passed and recognized. Then, the inter-port match between Hong Kong and Shanghai, the readmission of Midushixi, and three cases concerning the lease term of the venue were discussed. Finally, the Police Club Ju Bi proposed a temporary motion. All representatives present sincerely consulted and passed it satisfactorily. Chairman Yi read the Shanghai Western Union's letter of the 12th of last month, reiterating that they had no objection to extending the time by ten minutes for the inter-port match between Hong Kong and Shanghai to be held in Shanghai this year, requesting to send a team to meet during Christmas or the Lunar New Year. After the letter was read out, the opinions of the representatives were sought. Chen Hanming, the representative of the South China Club, said, "Given the current environment, it is still difficult for the South China Club to send personnel to participate." Ju Bi, the representative of the Police Club, said, "The inter-port match can wait until early spring next year." Chairman Bi, seeing that the committee members had a wait-and-see attitude, consulted the representatives of the Army and Navy, hoping that they could express their opinions, but both representatives said they had nothing to say. Chairman Bi, after learning that the proposal to send a team to Shanghai during the Christmas period was difficult to fulfill, then announced, "Within the possible scope, a team will be sent to fulfill the agreement during the Lunar New Year next year." The police representative first seconded the proposal, and the case was passed. The two matches, one to go and one to return, which had been arranged once before, were also implicitly cancelled.

Finance Export Bills of Exchange are Being Cashed Out in a Steady Stream, There is a Disparity between Supply and Demand, and the British and American Exchange Markets are Relaxing Non-Stop 51

Yesterday's foreign exchange market conditions: HSBC's listed prices did not rise or fall. The situation in the British and American exchange grey market was still loose, all because the "扒者" (market manipulators) were weak and the supply exceeded the demand. This is because people now generally believe that there is a major turning point in the situation, reversing the past style and tending to throw off/sell. This is due to the fact that the overseas British and American mutual exchange rate, the US to the UK rose by one and a half points from before the holiday, resulting in a divergence in the British and American situation. The UK was tight at 0.15625, while the US was strong at 0.3125. Subsequently, foreign telegrams from Hong Kong, etc., and exporters successively sold, and foreign banks such as Chase Bank and Chinese banks also sold positions, so the situation was uniformly loose and hard. However, although British banks were favorable and absorbed together with Japanese banks, it once returned to equilibrium, but it could not be maintained for long due to the disparity between the many and the few. As a result, the closing price was 4 and 625 and 7.8125, the loosest price of the day, 0.046875 looser than before the holiday and 0.15625 harder for the US. As for the future trend, there is no difference with the spot market. Trading in the morning was still strong, 0.0625, for 3 pence and 8125, for 1875 longer for US spot.

Chinese Merchants in Hong Kong are Still Selling

In the early morning, the London big bill, near term was long 375, far term rose 625, New York silver price rose 1.125, London gold was stable, exchange rates were even for UK to US, Shanghai, and France, and US was high for UK by 1.5, long for Shanghai by 5, and big 625 for France. The above were all settled according to the closure before the holiday. The Central Bank's listed exchange rates were the same as before. The bank opened the spot selling price in the morning, British gold was 4 and 5625, US exchange rate was 7.6875, which was slightly tighter for UK than the previous close by 0.015625, and slightly looser for US by 0.03125. This was due to the rise in the US and British exchange rates. After opening, the market trend became loose due to the successive sales by exporters and foreign telegrams from Hong Kong, etc., and foreign banks also had a strong willingness to sell. Exporters and Hong Kong telegrams sold spot British gold to foreign HSBC, etc. for 4 and 625, and then Hong Kong telegrams and certain banks such as Foreign Belgium-China and Chase Bank sold spot US exchange rates to money changers and foreign firms for 7.75 and 8.25. HSBC's listed prices were unchanged, and the silver balancing tax was announced to be one and a half points higher. After this, the British Bank and Right came to absorb, and the Japanese bank (Zhengjin Bank) also followed up and settled. Therefore, the situation once became tight. The British Bank and Right and Zhengjin Bank settled the spot British gold of foreign banks for 4 and 5625, and the spot US exchange rate for 7.75. Then, Chinese banks came to sell, and Hong Kong came to sell again, so the situation became more difficult. Chinese banks and foreign telegrams sold spot British gold to foreign banks for 4 and 625, and spot US exchange rate for 7.8125. Later, speculators sold the US exchange rate for November to foreign banks for 7.6875. Extended to the noon close, the bank's spot selling price, British gold was 4 and 625, US exchange rate was 7.8125, the current month was the same as the spot market, and the November British gold was 4 and 5625, and the US exchange rate was 7.6875. As a result, compared to before the holiday (i.e. Monday this week), both the current and future British exchange rates were loose by 0.046875, and the US exchange rates were all hard by 0.15625. Hong Kong Merchants are Watching, The Gold Price is Falling More Fiercely, Once Breaking the 4,000 Yuan Mark 53

Yesterday's spot gold grey market continued to decline, and the downward trend was even fiercer. It once broke into the 4,000 yuan mark before the evening close. This was because there was a certain atmosphere in the market, which led to the foreign exchange rate becoming looser. Therefore, the bullish thinking on gold was extraordinarily pessimistic. At the same time, Hong Kong merchants showed poor digestion and needed to stop abruptly, unlike the crazy swallowing and indiscriminate acceptance of the past few days. This newspaper once predicted that the main factor for the gold price to fall into the 4,000 yuan mark was also. Furthermore, some retail bulls also came to the market to close their positions, so the market showed a scattered and weak atmosphere. However, although there were many twists and turns in the middle, there was no fear of raising prices at all, and on the contrary, selling was extremely easy to fall, and the downward trend could not be stopped, and there was still fear that there would be no rebound in the future for the time being. In the past, the market opened weakly in the morning to 4,045 yuan. Subsequently, due to the loosening of foreign exchange and the emergence of a certain gold number bull and the securities gang following the sale, it was pressed down slightly to 4,012 yuan. Later, due to the disappearance of buyers, it broke the 4,000 yuan mark. Trading was still strong, about 1,000 taels. Silver building ornaments were listed for 5 yuan less, and customs gold, etc. were still stable.

Spot Gold Fell 53 Yuan

Since the morning, every bar (10 taels) initially opened with weak popularity. A certain gold number, etc. had a supply intention. The opening price was 8 yuan less than before the holiday (i.e. Monday this week). A certain gold number sold 20 taels to the securities gang, with the price being 4,045 yuan. After opening, it was heard that foreign exchange was loose and the situation was weak again. Sellers came one after another, and a certain gold number had a strong willingness to sell, and continued to fall by 15 yuan. A certain gold number sold 30 taels to the same industry, for 4,030 yuan. After this, a certain securities gang also started a selling trend, immediately selling more than 100 taels, and then pressing down 18 yuan again. The securities gang sold 20 taels to the silver building gang, with the price being 4,012 yuan. Subsequently, the foreign exchange turned tight, which stimulated people's hearts. In addition, a certain securities gang stopped selling and reversed. It soon returned to a high of 16 yuan. Money changers did 20 taels of mutual business, with the price being 4,028 yuan. Then, a certain gold number and silver building gang took the opportunity to sell, and once again fell to 4,015 yuan. Later, because a certain securities gang still had a buying interest, and a certain money changer also came to follow up, it was pulled up by 20 yuan again. Soviet Consulate Closed, All Matters Entrusted to the Norwegian Consul for Care, Procedures for Foreigners to Go to the Soviet Union All Under Norwegian Consulate, Consulates in Tianjin and Peiping Also Closed Simultaneously 65

According to Continental News, it was learned yesterday (9th) that all affairs of the Soviet Consulate in Shanghai have been entrusted to the Norwegian Consul-General, Mr. Niutecheng, for care. It is noted that the Soviet Consulate moved from the temporary building on Shanzhong Road to the official building at No. 20 Huangpu Beach ten days ago. However, since Soviet Consul Konstantinnov, accompanied by Vice-Consul Qiming and Consular Secretary Kolomeizev, took a boat to Japan on September 24, the Soviet Consulate has been empty. The consulate building is currently being looked after by Shaliyev. Although the purpose of Konstantinnov and others going to Tokyo has not been disclosed, it is generally believed that they may have been sent to Japan to complete the preparatory technical work for the recent ceasefire between the Soviet Union and Japan on the Outer Mongolian border. It is widely believed that after they complete their mission in Tokyo, they will set off directly for Moscow.

Norwegian Consul Takes Over Everything

According to the China Press, a senior official of the Norwegian Consulate stated last night (10th) that the Norwegian Consulate-General has taken over the consular duties of Soviet citizens in Shanghai since a few days ago, and has notified Soviet citizens that they must apply to the Norwegian Consulate-General for passports and other matters in the future. When asked about the reason for this move, the official said that he only knew that he had received instructions from the Norwegian government to take care of Soviet interests in Shanghai, and that he would know more after receiving further notice. It is also reported that there are currently no responsible Soviet consular officials in Shanghai, as the consulate staff left for the Soviet Union two weeks ago. Therefore, foreigners who wish to travel through the Soviet Union in the future must go through various procedures at the Norwegian Consulate-General.

Rumored to Affect Soviet-Japanese Relations

According to foreign sources, the Soviet government, due to different opinions with Japan on the China issue, is becoming increasingly hostile and has decided to close the consulates in Shanghai, Tianjin, and Beiping, and entrust the interests of Russian expatriates to the Norwegian consuls in the above-mentioned places for management. In the occupied areas of China, only one consulate is still set up in Harbin. According to inquiries from reliable sources in the diplomatic circles by the reporter yesterday morning, it has been confirmed.

It is learned that the Soviet and Norwegian Consulates in Shanghai suddenly received instructions from Moscow and Oslo on the 9th of this month, respectively, entrusting all diplomatic affairs of the Soviet Consulate in Shanghai to the Norwegian Consulate in Shanghai for management. As a result, after a meeting between the personnel of the two consulates, the diplomatic affairs of the Soviet Consulate were entrusted to the Norwegian Consulate for agency from the day before yesterday. After this news spread, all parties considered it important, and some even regarded it as a sign of the future international situation. Therefore, some foreign diplomats observed that this decision by the Soviet Union's diplomatic action may open up a new path, or at least its diplomatic policy towards the Far East may be re-adjusted. Therefore, they are all closely watching its future development. According to reliable sources, although the Soviet Union is not a signatory country to the Nine-Power Treaty and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, it abides by the spirit of the two and firmly safeguards China's sovereignty, independence, and territorial integrity. Recently, the Japanese side's request for the Soviet Union to stop aiding China has been sternly rejected by the Soviet government. In view of the increase in troops by both the Soviet Union and Japan on the Mongolian-Manchurian border, it is deeply believed that the temporarily eased Soviet-Japanese relations may become tense again, and the ceasefire agreement on the Mongolian-"Manchukuo" border will fall into the same fate as the Zhanggufeng ceasefire.

US Amends Neutrality Act, Opinions of American僑 in Shanghai, Regarding the Matter of US Ships Not Being Allowed to Approach Shanghai, Will Telegraph Washington to Urge Consideration of the Facts 66

If President Roosevelt does so, it is reasonable to expect that Shanghai will be included in the list of ports of belligerent countries, and Tianjin may also be included in it, because the surrounding areas of Shanghai and Tianjin are all in the Japanese-occupied areas. According to a survey conducted by the Association last spring, there has been a significant decrease in the number of Chinese students studying in the United States who are studying social sciences that are less practical than before, especially political science, while the number of students studying various engineering subjects is the largest, including 69 who specialize in aviation. This is because what China needs are engineering military students and technical experts.

According to the English-language Greater Shanghai Evening Post, Japanese maritime authorities have taken a series of puzzling actions since this year, seizing ships without giving reasons and detaining them directly at Zhoujiazui. Japanese Side Has Another Clever Explanation for Withdrawing from Zhongshan County, Saying That It Is Showing Respect for Sun Yat-sen and Trusts That the People of the County Can Govern Themselves 72

The Japanese naval spokesman said at the press briefing last night that the Japanese army withdrew from Zhongshan County, Guangdong, on the Double Tenth Festival to show respect for Prime Minister Sun because Zhongshan County is Prime Minister Sun's hometown. The Japanese army's occupation and withdrawal from Zhongshan County, due to the speed of action, has given the Chinese army a heavy blow, so the Japanese army has achieved a "brilliant victory." The spokesman continued, "There is another reason for the Japanese army to withdraw from Zhongshan County, that is, it trusts that the people of the county will be able to follow Prime Minister Sun's instructions, implement autonomy, and move forward on the path of anti-communism and pro-Japanese from now on. However, if Zhongshan County becomes a base for communism or is used for the Chinese army, the Japanese army will attack the area again and punish the local people." As of today, the Chinese army has never admitted to abandoning Zhongshan County. A Reuters dispatch from Zhongshan said that Zhang Huichang, the commander of the Chinese army there, was still commanding the army while wounded by shrapnel, which shows the intensity of the battle. According to a Chinese dispatch from Guilin on the 9th, the Japanese troops invading Zhongshan were severely attacked by the Chinese army and were blocked near Youqi, forming a confrontation. Zhongshan County is still in the hands of the Chinese army, which shows that the explanation of the Japanese naval spokesman has a clever effect.

On the 10th, the Japanese newspapers covered up the failure of the Japanese army to invade Changsha, saying that "the Japanese army used clever tactics to severely damage the party army in the Ninth War Zone, established brilliant results, and returned to the base with success." This decision is the reason for the Japanese side's statement to withdraw from Zhongshan County, which is similar to its clever action and is also to cover up its defeat.

Rice Prices Continue to Plummet Due to Abundant Arrivals 74

More Than 7,000 Packages Reached the Market, Prices of Various Goods Fell by 2 to 3 Yuan

The late rice in the rice-producing areas of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, including Wuhu, Jiaxing, Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, and Changshu, has been harvested abundantly, and it is being transported to Shanghai for sale. The amount of rice and grain transported to Shanghai by land and water routes is increasing daily, and the inventory of rice shops in Shanghai is gradually increasing. The entire supply of staple food can be guaranteed, and the public's concerns have been dispelled. The business of rice shops has become quiet, and there are few retail buyers. However, all rice and grain transported to Shanghai from various places must hold so-called "transport permits," and they are only allowed to be transported to Shanghai after local taxes and levies have been collected on each stone. Otherwise, they will be detained. Therefore, the procedures for rice and grain to reach Shanghai are more complicated than in the past. The rice market was closed on the National Day holiday, and it reopened as usual at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. The rice registered by cargo owners with the Rice Market Management Committee for consignment reached 7,620 packages, an increase of more than 2,200 packages compared with the rice registered for consignment on the 9th. Due to the large influx of goods and weak digestion, cargo owners are eager to sell, resulting in a drop of three yuan per stone for new japonica rice, with the highest price being 28 yuan per stone, and a drop of two yuan per stone for indica rice, with the highest price being 17 yuan per stone. Five or six boats from Hexia came yesterday, carrying more than seventy packages of steamed buns. According to an official of the Management Committee, the Market Management Committee is scheduled to convene a plenary committee meeting the day after tomorrow to prepare for the promulgation of the temporary regulations on market asset purchase, which were revised and approved by the seven rice industry groups at a joint meeting, on the 16th, and to discuss other proposals from various colleagues.

French Concession Authorities Crack Down on German Intelligence Operations, Carefully Issue Various Licenses, Paying Attention to Those Impersonating German Jewish Refugees 75

The French Concession Municipal Council has now decided that applicants from German residents in the concession who are applying for building permits and business licenses must be carefully issued these licenses only after the authorities have investigated and considered the applications. The Municipal Council yesterday re-issued a notice to various departments within the council, ordering them to pay attention to German intelligence operations within the concession in order to reduce them. Due to this order, all residents holding German passports, including Jewish refugees who fled Germany due to political reasons, have been affected. However, the intention of the French authorities is not to restrict well-behaved German residents, so building and business licenses will be issued if, after individual examination, they are indeed deemed harmless. Since the influx of German Jewish refugees seeking asylum in Shanghai, no fewer than several thousand have opened businesses and made a living in the French Concession. The French authorities have expressed that they will not make things difficult for German Jewish residents who are settling down and working. However, it is heard that some non-Jewish Germans engaged in intelligence work are secretly adding a red "J" mark to their passports (note that the French authorities issue German Jewish passports with a "J" mark) in an attempt to impersonate German Jews. Therefore, the German authorities have no choice but to pay close attention to the investigation of German Jewish residents.

The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial sectors' ten-day term transfers are approaching. Regarding the expiring credit loans, the shops agreed to the requests of various industries and have agreed to accommodate them. Overseas Interest Rate Market, Considered Stable

Considering the Hardships of Postal Workers, Subsidy Measures 80

Postmen Refuse to Accept Women, Increased Fees for Southeast Asian Airmail

The entire staff of the Shanghai Postal Administration previously requested subsidies from the bureau due to rising prices and difficult living conditions to maintain their current livelihoods. Subsequently, the bureau director, Mr. Cha Peilin, telegraphed the Kunming Postal Administration to explain the high cost of living in Shanghai and the difficulties faced by postal workers. Starting in July of this year, a uniform increase of 7.5 yuan per person per month was granted from grade B postal workers to letter carriers. Now, the Kunming Postal Administration, in consideration of the special environment in Shanghai and to alleviate the difficulties faced by postal workers, has ordered the Shanghai Postal Administration to further stipulate the following monthly subsidy measures for postal workers: (1) 1 yuan per month for postal workers, (2) 7.5 yuan per month for letter carriers, etc., (3) 3-4 yuan per month for laborers, depending on the hardship of each person's work (including the previous increase of 7.5 yuan). It is heard that these measures will be implemented starting this month.

Refuse to Accept Women

The General Postal Administration previously issued a notice stating that if the number of female employees in each administration exceeds 5% of the total number, no more female employees will be recruited in the future. The women's circles in Shanghai, believing that this would harm the future of women's careers, specifically telegraphed Madam Chiang and others, requesting the protection of women's rights. It is learned that after the Shanghai Postal Administration recruited junior postal workers on June 4th of this year, it stated that the number of female employees in the bureau had reached 6% of the total number. The second recruitment of junior postal workers, to be held on the 22nd of this month, will not accept any female applicants. However, the bureau currently has a total of 3,080 letter carrier employees, of which only 39 are female, and the number has not reached 5% of the total number. In addition to fighting for their rights with the bureau, the female employees are also appealing to the outside world for strong social assistance.

Southeast Asian Airmail

The Shanghai Postal Administration announced on the 11th that, starting immediately, for airmail destined for Indochina, British India, Malaya, Siam, Burma, India, and Iran, carried by British Royal Air Force planes departing from Hong Kong, the required additional airmail surcharge will be increased by 65 cents in national currency for every five grams. Airmail arriving from various western regions, carried by the company's Hanoi to Hong Kong segment of the plane, will also be increased in the same way. The notice is issued for general knowledge.

According to the Shanghai Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, the exchange fee for Shantou postal remittances has been changed as follows: from now on, in addition to the one cent exchange fee, an additional two cent water subsidy fee will be charged for each yuan. The amount of remittances in each place will depend on the local situation.

Explanation of President's "The Logic of Action" (Continued) 82

— Kong Lingkan

The driving force of "action" is sincerity, and the expression of "action" lies in creation, progress, construction, and the completion of the Three People's Principles revolution. The ultimate goal of "action" is "to sacrifice oneself for righteousness and to give up life for justice." The motivation of revolution is to save people, and the duty of revolution is to practice benevolence. To practice benevolence and obtain benevolence is the result of revolution. At the same time, scientific methods must be used, and attention must be paid to the four major elements of "action."

(1) There must be a starting point, a point for me to start from. Climbing high starts from below, traveling far starts from nearby. One cannot start beyond one's level and must start from the grassroots.

(2) There must be order. Plan thoroughly, set steps, and recognize the time, environment, and content of events to prepare in advance.

(3) There must be a purpose. Identify the purpose and do not stop until it is achieved.

(4) It must be continuous. Revolutionary action is just a plain and simple behavior, without the need for ingenious methods or speculative attempts.

After we understand the four major elements of "action," we can act, and only by being able to act can we talk about revolution.

Premier Sun Yat-sen invented the truth that "knowing is difficult, acting is easy" and said, "Human beings have different degrees of understanding: those who know and understand in advance, those who know and understand later, and those who do not know or understand at all. For those who know and understand in advance, after studying and understanding clearly, as long as everyone believes in them, obeys them, and follows them to do it earnestly, they can act immediately." It can be seen that no matter what, as long as someone can believe in and obey the guidance of those who know and understand in advance and do it, nothing is impossible to do. President Chiang Kai-shek inherits Premier Sun Yat-sen's legacy to guide our party members and the masses in revolution, which is to guide those who know later with those who know in advance and to awaken those who understand later with those who understand in advance. As long as we can believe in and obey President Chiang Kai-shek's leadership, and move forward courageously with an indomitable and decisive spirit, we will surely complete the revolution, reach the broad road, and discover a bright future. This is self-evident. For thousands of years, our people have been dominated by the argument that "knowing is not difficult, acting is difficult," which has made us weak and unmotivated. We only know how to talk without taking action. The path of self-cultivation, family regulation, governance, and peace mentioned by the sages is often regarded as a theory that cannot be put into practice, thus making China, a country with a vast territory, abundant resources, and a large population, lag behind in everything. Not only can we not compete with the world's countries, but we are still being ravaged by island barbarians today, which is very painful. The reason for this is that the inability to act is the root cause. Japan stole the remnants of Yangming's philosophy of "extending conscience" and put it into practice. Since the Meiji Restoration, naval officers, army officers, from the Emperor to the soldiers, and educated citizens have all taken the three words "extending conscience" as the philosophical foundation of their national spirit, cultivating a spirit of chivalry, loyalty to the Emperor, and patriotism. Therefore, today they can be strong in the world and even dare to invade China, the source of their national spirit's philosophical foundation. Sun Tzu said, "Know the enemy and know yourself, and you will not be defeated in a hundred battles." Now that we are fighting for justice, we must first study the reasons for the decline of the Chinese nation and the spirit of Japan's founding. Once we understand these, we can know the enemy. But we must also look back at ourselves, find the key, and then act, and then we can win a hundred battles. Premier Sun Yat-sen created the doctrine of "knowing is difficult, acting is easy," and President Chiang Kai-shek used this doctrine to enlighten us. Why don't we quickly follow the purpose, track, and system, and continue to act? Do we want to willingly "sit idle" and wait for death? If everyone can obey President Chiang Kai-shek's leadership and act, it will be as easy as turning one's hand to turn China from weak to strong. Now that the country is in trouble and a strong enemy is rampaging, as long as we are determined to believe that "the final victory will belong to us," and follow President Chiang Kai-shek to act, overcome the environment with perseverance, not be arrogant in victory, not be discouraged in defeat, and continue to "act" one after another, using the truth of "action" to strive for glory, set a firm determination, and act with enthusiasm according to our beliefs, then the war of resistance will surely be won, the country will surely be built, and the future of the party and the country will be limitless. A small island is not worth mentioning. (End)

Husband and Wife Take Poison in the Chunjiang Inn 86

At 1 PM on the 9th, a Ningbo man, Liang Zhu, 30 years old, and his wife, Liang Zhang, 25 years old, checked into room 10 of the Chunjiang No. 1 Inn, 309 Caishi Street, French Concession. They stayed overnight on the 10th, but unexpectedly, the couple committed suicide together that night. Zhang took poison, while Liang hanged himself on the bed frame. It was not until 1 PM yesterday that the tea server, Xu Xiaodi (36 years old, from Minhang), saw that Liang and his wife had not gotten up and knocked on the door, but there was no response. After prying open the door and entering, he discovered that the couple had committed suicide. Zhang was lying on the bed, barely breathing, while Liang's body was still warm. He immediately took him down and reported to the French Police, who sent detectives to investigate. A suicide note was left behind, and they were sent to Guangci Hospital for rescue. Zhang died two hours after being admitted to the hospital due to severe poisoning. The hospital notified the police station, and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home for an autopsy. The Special Court will be requested to send personnel to examine the body today. The reason for the suicide is said to be economic reasons.

Large Parcels to America Must Be Posted One Week in Advance 87

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 1579: Due to the current situation, the number of ship voyages has been reduced, and all parcels sent to America are extremely crowded, making it difficult to load and export them. If merchants have large parcels to be sent to America, they must post them one week before the bureau's sealing date, or first submit a letter to the bureau's parcel receiving group for registration, so that the space on the ship can be reserved for loading on schedule. This notice is hereby issued for general knowledge.

French Police Department Strictly Arrests Hooligans, Dozens Arrested in Recent Days 88

The French Concession Police Department, in view of the rampant hooliganism in the concession, which endangered public security, sent detectives to investigate. It was confirmed that hooligans were wreaking havoc everywhere. For example, when a resident's baby died, they demanded a fixed price of five yuan. When a shop opened, they even led a crowd to extort several to dozens of yuan. Other wedding and funeral celebrations and posted notices were immediately exploited by hooligan leaders from various sections to extort protection money, which was deeply hated by the citizens. Therefore, the police department specially formed a group responsible for cleaning up. After several days of major arrests, it is heard that dozens of people have been arrested, and the hooligans have disappeared in recent days and dare not cause trouble.

The Hollywood gambling den on Yu Road, which is known as one of the top gold-selling dens in Shanghai, has been greatly affected, and the number of gamblers at night has decreased, causing business to plummet. Recently, it has been in a state of collapse. It is heard that the den was suddenly robbed by bandits some time ago, resulting in heavy losses. Therefore, the internal situation has been even more in decline in recent days.

Flying Thief Captured Again, Claims to Have Reformed and Changed His Ways, Ordered to be Detained for Further Investigation and Verification 91

Wang Zhaorong, a well-known flying thief from Huzhou, 28 years old, specializes in stealing valuables from the residences of foreign merchants in the British and French Concessions. He is able to climb over walls and eaves, hence the name "flying thief." He was previously arrested and sent to court, where he was sentenced to a heavy sentence. He had been missing for a long time. Recently, the residences of foreign merchants in the Western District of the French Concession have been reporting the theft of large amounts of valuables. The French Police Department ordered detectives to investigate and arrest him. It was recently learned by Detective Chief Xin that Wang was hiding in room 11 of the Hai Dongchun Inn in Yude Lane, Yunnan Road, British Concession. They then joined forces with the Public Police Department and sent detectives to arrest Wang and brought him back to the French Police Department. Yesterday afternoon, he was sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court and interrogated by Judge Zhang Minsheng. Police lawyer Yuan Jiahuang stated that the defendant's theft case was not yet fully investigated and requested a postponement for further questioning. Wang confessed that he had committed theft before, but had now reformed and changed his ways and was making a living by performing opera. The court verified his confession and ordered him to be detained for further investigation and verification at a later date.

To whom it may concern: We, Weng Guangxin, Weng Guangyong, Weng Cai-shi, and Weng Guiying, the owners of the Jiatai Clothing Store, hereby state that our younger brothers, Guangzheng and Guangzhe, colluded with our father's concubine and took advantage of the situation to embezzle a large sum of money from the store over the years. Therefore, after a family meeting, they were relieved of their duties as assistant managers, and Guangxin was appointed as the manager. All co-owners jointly took over the management to thoroughly investigate the fraudulent accounts to rectify the situation and protect the joint property. On September 28th, when Guangxin and others took over the store affairs according to law and ordered the handover of account books, Guangzheng instigated store employees to forcibly open the account box, intending to steal the account books. Guangxin and others stopped them, but to no avail. Therefore, they took the store employees and the account box to the police station to file a complaint. Unexpectedly, Guangzheng instead instigated the store employees to falsely accuse Guangxin and others of robbing the account box. After investigation, the police station found the accusations to be false and that the matter involved a domestic dispute between brothers. They released them and refused to accept the case. There is a record of this. However, Guangzheng, instigated by others, did not hesitate to turn against his own family. On the 4th of this month, while Guangxin and others were working in the store, he falsely reported to the police station, falsely accusing them of obstructing his freedom. Although the police station summoned Guangxin and others to the court, the court did not prosecute them because the matter involved a civil family dispute. Now, five days have passed, and yesterday we saw a section in the *Shen Bao*'s local news titled "Brothers Sued for Disputing Clothing Store Manager Position." Many of the facts are inaccurate. The report stated that they "swarmed into the store, disregarding the situation, forcibly took over the store, and drove Weng Guangzheng out of the store." However, Guangxin and others have always been working in their own store, so there was no such thing as swarming into the store. On the 4th of this month, when Guangzheng falsely reported to the police station, Guangxin and others never quarreled with him before or after the incident. The landlords of the second house and the neighbors all witnessed this. How could there be such a thing as driving him out of the store? Moreover, in the police station and the court, he himself never made such a statement. This is evidenced by the written records. The report also stated that "French police officers rushed to No. 26, Taihe Lane, Baier Road, and arrested Weng Guangxin and the other three people." This is even more untrue. According to the facts, Guangxin and the other three people were summoned while they were in their own store. There was no such thing as reported in the news. This news is clearly inaccurate. To avoid misunderstandings from the outside world, we kindly request that you write to the newspaper to request a correction to reveal the truth. We are writing on their behalf and hope that your newspaper will publish this letter in the "Correspondence" section to make a correction. We pray for this. Respectfully addressed to Mr. Chief Editor of *Shen Bao*, Lawyer Shao Shengzu, October 9th.
