Free Talk

The Destruction of Sennacherib 96

— By Byron, translated by Pinpin

The Assyrian came down like the wolf on the fold,

And his cohorts were gleaming in purple and gold;

And the sheen of their spears was like stars on the sea,

When the blue wave rolls nightly on deep Galilee.

Like the leaves of the forest when Summer is green,

That host with their banners at sunset were seen:

Like the leaves of the forest when Autumn hath blown,

That host on the morrow lay withered and strown.

For Death breathed in the face of the foe as he passed;

And the tents were all silent, the banners alone,

And his breath withered eyes.

And their hearts but once heaved, and for ever grew still!

And there lay the steed with his nostril all wide,

But through it there rolled not the breath of his pride:

And the foam of his gasping lay white on the turf,

And cold as the spray of the rock-beaten surf.

And there lay the rider distorted and pale,

With the dew on his brow, and the rust on his mail:

And the tents were all silent, the banners alone,

The lances unlifted, the trumpet unblown.

And the widows of Ashur are loud in their wail,

And the idols are broke in the temple of Baal;

And the might of the Gentile, unsmote by the sword,

Hath melted like snow in the glance of the Lord!

(Original title: The Destruction of Sennacherib)

Japan Today in the Age of Substitutes (Part 1) 97

— Written by Midorikawa Eiko, translated by Wang Sanjie

A rickshaw puller who hasn't eaten enough…

Dazzling wooden clogs

"Let's call a car home right away!"

That's what I thought in my heart after the train arrived in Tokyo, so I got off the train immediately and rushed outside the station. Because I hadn't seen my parents for two years!

But strangely! The cars that used to crowd in front of the station are now nowhere to be seen, replaced only by some dirty rickshaws.

Helplessly, I had to take a rickshaw. But I don't know if it was because I was so eager to see my parents, or because the rickshaw puller was sick or hadn't eaten enough? It made me feel that the rickshaw was moving so slowly through the streets and alleys, inching forward step by step.

Oh, so many wooden clogs!

"I'm almost dizzy. I never thought that even those gentlemen in gorgeous Western clothes would wear wooden clogs, kicking and stomping on the sidewalks. I remember that about fifty years ago, a certain Mr. Lefcadio Hearn (i.e., Koizumi Yakumo), a Japanophile, praised the noise of wooden clogs as 'Japanese mysticism.' Is the government now trying to exhibit this 'national essence' to the world? But everyone knows that wartime Japan doesn't have enough leather to make leather shoes, and even Mr. Hearn, if he were still alive, would frown and shake his head in dissatisfaction at this 'anachronism'!"

…Mr. Ikeda Shōhin… the leader… of wartime material control… wants to buy a carriage and a coachman…

I heard a radio station broadcasting this intermittently when I changed trains in Shinjuku.

The "New Morality" of Aggressors

A daughter coming home after two years should make her mother laugh with joy. However, my return home didn't make my mother happy, but instead made her cry, because she was thinking of her son on the battlefield in China.

In the evening, she muttered everything in front of her daughter; cursing the constant rise in prices, the increasing layers of taxes... and even complaining that the hospital gave her ineffective medicine... Now they can only eat whale meat instead of pork and beef... She said that the two gold teeth she originally had were also taken out and replaced with a kind of "synthetic gold" with a strange name. And according to her, she felt that everything tasted bland ever since...

——Ah! "S.F.", that bad thing! She exclaimed suddenly as if she had just thought of it. Then she angrily told me. (Originally, "S.F." is an abbreviation for a kind of substitute cotton cloth). She said: That bad thing, it's uncomfortable to wear, it's not durable, but it's very expensive! Of course, she said: the ladies of those "Patriotic Women's Association" and "National Defense Women's Association" can wear those pure white aprons made of it to show off! But what about some women who have to work all day? Sigh, I have to buy at least two aprons for my mother every month! Think, aprons are like this, clothes, what about them? What about everything else to wear? What a huge expense! Do the Chinese also use this annoying "S.F." or even worse things?

——No, I immediately replied to her: The Chinese do not lack cotton cloth!

——China is a country that "has" things! Father suddenly interjected: And Japan is a country that "lacks" things. That's why this war started.

I was about to refute this excuse of fascist aggressors, but mother opened her mouth:

——A few days ago, I went to Ito for a trip, and I don't know what kind of hot spring this is? But it's so strange, the towel made of S.F. that I used only for the first time, dissolved in the bath, and, ah...

Seemingly like a virgin, suddenly mother blushed and couldn't continue. (Japan has a custom of mixed bathing for men and women, using only a towel to cover the lower body, whether at home or in public bathhouses.)

——It doesn't matter, Mom! This is the "new morality" of Japanese aggressors! I said, stabbing out like a sharp knife.

——Bastard! Father suddenly got angry: You... you, even your soul has been assimilated by the Chinese...

The Mailbox is Crying

Iron! Iron!! Iron!!!

The whole of Japan is boiling over with the demand for iron.

One day, my brother sent us a letter from the front line in Central China. The letter contained only a few sentences in between:

——...Recently, I don't know why, the letters from Japan are always so damp that even the words are not very clear. Is our military postal service now so bad?

Dear brother, I wrote back to tell him: In your motherland, people now have nothing to give you who are fighting abroad except tears. Now, everything is surprisingly expensive! But tears are becoming less and less valuable. Day after day, desperately looking to the west, mothers cry, wives cry, children cry, and even the newly emerged female postmen cry for their husbands who will never return, and even the iron mailboxes cry... Ah, that's right! Brother, you still don't know, do you? There are 100,000 mailboxes in the whole of Japan, 20,000 of which are made of iron, and a month ago someone removed the 20,000 iron ones and replaced them with non-metallic ones. So as soon as it rains, they cry immediately - and the letters inside get wet. Dear brother! You must know: in Japan, 20,000 mailboxes are crying, and in China, those old iron 20,000, have already become bombs and made countless innocent neighbors cry!...

Sea Love 98

— Lin Hao

The mighty and majestic spirit, like a reckless wild bull, using its horns to charge fiercely at the heel of the cliffs, without rest or tranquility; this irritability and ambition has always been a trace that I have found difficult to forget since my childhood.

I love even more the summit of the shady ridge near the sea, blowing in the wind, looking far into the vast expanse of white silk, rolling its huge and incomparably large body, slowly and quickly opening its mouth, rolling its wings, tossing over, as if swallowing me in one gulp; I immediately feel a long and comfortable breath of fresh air coming out of my heart; everything becomes pleasant and refreshing, no matter how great your melancholy mistakes or memories are, they will all turn into nothing!

Because I love the sea, my mother repeatedly taught me:

"Child! Go to the sea less, the sea is a terrible monster!"

I am stubborn. I didn't remember my mother's words; I still lingered by the sea.

At night, I followed the darkness and quietly went out of the house. Starlight pointed to the fields, and from time to time I would trample on a few small puddles full of water, making a TATA sound, I ignored everything. For the sake of the sea, I am willing to endure grievances. Listening to the old frogs croaking, walking the familiar road. I hoped, and began to lie down on the beach, watching the cloud shadows dyed by the seawater.

Three or two black dots, flapping heavy wings, flying by the sea, shimmering with silver light reflected by the moonlight, that is the chase of bats and gray birds.

The world is quiet, but the sea is not quiet, the shouts of the Volga boatmen; majestic, tidy, rhythmically chanting for the people in dreams to enjoy. But they are all dead, they cannot hear the song of the sea at night; only I am fortunate enough to boast of myself.

If the night wind hadn't woken me up, (it was cold) I wouldn't have been so reluctant to leave this great sea.

Just like that, I often warmed my bed only when the watchman was striking three o'clock.

Facing the morning breeze, watching the free seagulls chasing the water fish, listening to the sound of the oars struggling out of the fishing boat; that is also a beautiful pencil sketch of the sea.

However, later, gradually, the whip of life shook behind my back, and I began to leave the paradise of my childhood. The environment, in turn, forged me into a city parasite.

It has been three years since I went to my childhood hometown, nor have I been to the Wusongkou that can be regarded as a memory; although I was in there, I was熏陶成像 a selfish, mean, and sordid hero by the high houses, the coal smoke of the big fire wheels, and its narrowness; but that could at least warm my lost old dreams!

What about now? I often dream of that mysterious and majestic sea.

Sea, I miss you! I want to swoop above you like a petrel, unafraid of the mourning of the diving birds, and regardless of the timidity of the penguins; come, you bring lightning and storms, I will bravely make a huge return.

On Short Works 99

— Chi Qiang

Recently, various newspaper supplements generally welcome short works. This is a common requirement of editors, and readers are even praying silently.

Short drafts are like short weapons, and short weapons may be the best weapons for hand-to-hand combat or street fighting. Long and lengthy writings, like a long snake array, sometimes inevitably suffer from "tail too big to wag."

If art is really to be worthy of being called "paper bullets," then these "paper bullets" should also be economical now, and these "paper bullets" should also be cherished. Although cherishing is not like the "Tongshanshe" so enthusiastically "cherishing written paper" for the seeds of reading to "call to heaven," in order to exert its effectiveness, it is better to be short than redundant, it is better to be precise than crude, it is better to be powerful than tired and numb, then shortness as shortness must also take on its responsibilities.

Someone once looked at a twenty-story skyscraper and felt dizzy, knowing how hard it is to stretch the neck, and it seems to be an exaggeration of life and a luxury of mankind; this may be an extreme statement. But in addition to dealing with myriad affairs every day (both physically and mentally), living in a streamlined life, this originally needs to be tasted with sufficient leisure. Therefore, encountering two small structures - such as a "Spanish-style" courtyard - will feel a sense of freshness.

The reason why short works are loved is probably this. We cannot throw away a stone and anchor the giant wheel of the times by our side; and we cannot excessively lengthen our lives, and we cannot but capture a little of the diverse shadow of the times, but we need a batch of short and meaningful things to entrust our hearts and entrust our bodies.

Human psychology is also very strange. New droplets stir up new ripples, and then fill a few satisfying waves; chasing ripples and searching for seven droplets from those waves, we feel even more fresh. But look at these fresh things, continuing, continuing, strung together one after another, like candle oil, the old ones as stepping stones, the tender ones flowing in those gaps.

Here, I hope for short, fine pieces to fill the gaps on the road of life!

Traveling in the World of Film History

The Origin of the Name Hollywood 100

— Pei Fei

Hollywood, the film city, the "Kingdom of Cinema" that tens of millions of people around the world are watching, the origin of its name is probably unknown to the general public, but they are happy to know. Here, let me tell you all about it.

If we divide the Hollywood area into east, south, west, and north, then its center is Cahuenga Avenue and Hollywood Boulevard. Cahuenga Avenue was originally a mountain road more than two hundred years ago. Going north from here for six miles, you can reach the city of Honiba Xiu and the Southant Plains of Self. This place is usually called "Cahuenga Pass", which was once a small mountain path passed by the Spanish expeditionary force of monks.

In 1770, when the old monk Qiu Pibiro. Sarah passed this path, because he was tired from walking, he temporarily rested in the shade of a tree, and accidentally swept his eyes to the distance, saw the oak tree growing there, could not help but exclaim in amazement, praising: "Holy Forest of the Cross" (Holly Wood of Cross)! As a result, people mistakenly thought that the origin of the name Hollywood came from here. ——Actually, it is wrong.

At that time, Hollywood was an uninhabited area. In 1855, the first house was built; "Hollywood Village", that name was only in 1887 later.

When Meijishi Kotto broke away from Spain, and the people of the whole country were happy, a young youth was living on a farm in Michigan, and this person was later the famous Holland. Uynnill Kokoqi. In 1880, after the death of his ex-wife, he married a girl named Tengda. Hattanal, soon after, he rode an Arabian horse across the continent and stopped at the Ross & Angiles area. In 1900, the product of the two of them died unfortunately, and in order to forget their sorrow, they moved to Hollywood, bought a farm of one hundred and sixty acres, and they planted a kind of tree called Holly on this farmland.

Hollywood, correctly speaking, comes from the word Holly. ——It refers to these holly trees, because holly trees are generally regarded as the cleanest things in the West.

In 1898, the first post office was established. Later, due to the rapid increase in population and the convenience of transportation, it was officially named a city by the government in 1903, and the first mayor elected was Sunfuwater. Riki.

In 1911, the first motion picture studio was built in Hollywood. After that, Hollywood became the center of the world's film industry, no, a kingdom of cinema.

Actress Song Dechuan Talks About: Practicing Stilt Skills and Fighting (Part 2) 101

— Recorded by Leng Fang

Anecdotes of an Entertainer

Three Years of Hard Work

Stilt skills and fighting are the basic skills of martial arts actresses, and the learning process is equally difficult without hard work. In the past, when I entered school at the age of fourteen, I first started practicing stilt skills: two wooden stilts were tied to my legs, and my feet were placed on them, only allowing force, and I had to practice for one or two hours every day. The first step: like a child learning to walk, groping against the wall, walking with a cane, after a few months, the gait was quite stable. The second step: standing dullly upright on a narrow stool, starting from one or two minutes, gradually increasing to be able to stand firmly for one hour, and it took nearly a year. The third step: standing on bricks, standing two tiles upright and dividing them on the ground, also starting from a few minutes, and after a year of work, slowly standing for one hour. The fourth step, running on a broomstick, tightly clamping a broomstick between the legs, moving slowly step by step, gradually changing from slow to fast, walking with fine steps inch by inch, after half a year. —This is used for running around the arena, and clamping the broomstick is a learning method that restricts walking wide steps. The basic skills of stilt work are considered complete only when walking and stopping are stable. In this way, working day and night under strict discipline, counting the time will be nearly three years, and for this reason, all the strength is in the toes, and very tight thick skin grows on it: now I usually like to wear shoes with higher heels, which is also a habit formed by practicing stilt work.

New Inventions

After learning stilt skills well, you must practice Baizi, somersaults, and general waist and leg skills to achieve considerable success, and then you can start fighting. The learning process of this skill is from simple to complex, focusing on speed. The teacher's instruction only pointed out one method, which should be practiced hard by oneself, and after a long time, you will be able to handle it with ease, and skillfully play out various ever-changing patterns. Therefore, this point can only be understood, and it is difficult to say how to learn it. I remember the teachers often said: "Art begins with method and ends with no method. If you can build a solid foundation, you will be able to exert it as you wish." These words are quite correct. Although my various fighting martial arts skills are not fully impressive, most of them come from arbitrary creation. As a result of the dedicated research in the past year, a total of eight sets of new fighting methods have been obtained, each set has twenty or thirty kinds, some simple and some complex, and no names have been decided yet. The only one that feels slightly satisfactory is one person dealing with three people, and playing the equal spears (usually only three spears) into a continuous ring, constantly floating in the air.

Greatest Wish

My greatest wish is to definitely go to Europe and America. At first, Qiao Ping, after seeing my fighting performance, praised me a lot and strongly urged me to go abroad to perform. Mr. Li Boyan of the drama school is a diplomat in Europe and also holds this view. Therefore, my wish is very firm, and sooner or later I will have to make this long journey. I know very well that my skills are still shallow, and I am even more unwilling to underestimate myself. Now I am only working hard, not interfering with other things, and I firmly believe that taking advantage of my youth and strength is an important period for me to strive for progress.

To all contributors: I am very grateful for your great works in September. The royalties have now been settled. Please prepare a sealed stamp and collect them from the accounting office of this library from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM on the 16th to 19th of this month. Also, Yan Chengxi, Zhi Bai, Hao Ran, Dai Ni, Boeing, Tian Ma, Paul, Meixiangshizhuren, Yujun, Zhi Yue, Yi An, Ke Yun Louzhu, Qiusheng, Yin Si, Li Tongyu, Zhi Yun, Lisa, Leng Fang, Dongcun Jushi, Beni, Man, Tongzhai Yuyi, Yang Liu, Jiao Chao, Liu Zhengzhu, please send the seal within three days to check and issue.

The Dictator Declared Stranded 102

— De Gang

The long-rumored Chaplin's talkie "The Dictator," which had been in production for more than half a year, has recently been suspended. The reason is that with the outbreak of the European war, the U.S. government feared causing various political disputes, so it advised Chaplin to stop filming. Chaplin himself also knew that the European war would greatly affect the film's sales, so he also agreed to postpone filming. However, according to him, once the war ends, he will continue the project and ensure its complete success, so as not to disappoint the audience's high expectations.

Since the news of the suspension spread, movie fans around the world have been greatly disappointed. To console the audience, Chaplin decided to film another light-hearted comedy. The theme has not yet been announced. Those who love Chaplin's works can rest assured, at least for now.

Anecdotes from the Peking Opera World 103

— Xu Yiyun

The Filial Piety and Righteousness of the Three Lius

It was often said in the past that "actors have no righteousness," and that these people perform all the virtues of loyalty, filial piety, chastity, and righteousness on stage, so they are disloyal, unfilial, unkind, and unrighteous in private. However, this statement cannot be generalized. There are bad ones, of course, but there are also many good people. I will now present three people who can serve as good role models for today's male and female actors. I hope that all the actors of today will pay attention. What is most strange is that these three all happen to be surnamed Liu, which is very different from the line in "A Monk's Revenge" where Liu Jin scolds the matchmaker Liu: "How can good people live together with such wretches?" It is evident that these three Lius are definitely not from the matchmaker Liu's family.

"Filial Piety and Righteousness" is originally the name of a play, which tells the story of Sun Shangxiang hearing the news of Liu Bei's death and throwing herself into the river, and then entering the palace to entrust a dream to Wu Guotai. However, what is described in this article is not the issue of the play. The so-called "Filial Piety and Righteousness of the Three Lius" refers to the filial piety of Liu Kuiguan, a famous painted-face actor, the righteousness of Liu Gansan, a famous clown actor, and the chastity of Liu Xikui, a famous female impersonator.

Kuiguan was from Licheng, Shandong. He studied under famous teachers such as Ge Wenyu, Fan Baoting, Li Zhonghua, and Wang Fulian, so he was able to perform all kinds of plays, including martial male roles, martial painted-face roles, male painted-face roles, and red-faced roles. In his prime, he performed for a long time in major cities of Henan Province and Xubeng area, and his reputation was excellent. In the tenth year of the Republic of China, he came to Shanghai and joined the Danggui First Stage, becoming famous immediately. Later, he performed at the Tianchan and other stages for a long time, so many people in Shanghai knew his name. Several years ago, a close friend of his, who was already a commander in Sichuan, invited Liu to Sichuan to form a troupe, so he left and never returned. It is said that his recent situation is quite good, and he gets along very well with people from all walks of life in Sichuan's military and political circles, and many people respect him for his character. The biggest reason is that the story of Liu cutting his flesh to treat his parents has long been well known, and in addition, this act actually came from someone in the acting world in recent times, so it is generally considered to be an unparalleled act of filial piety. Also, Liu is a member of the Hongmen Society, and he usually attaches great importance to the concept of righteousness. There are many fellow members in Sichuan, and the fact that he has been able to maintain his position there for a long time is not unrelated to this. (117) Chess Garden

Game 110: Bombarding the Enemy 104

— Devised by Zhu Mingyuan, a 13-year-old boy. Red goes first and wins.

The Moves of "Seven Captures of Meng Huo"

Pawn 3 advances to 4, General 6 advances to 1, Pawn 4 advances 1, General 6 retreats 1, Pawn 6 advances to 5, General 6 moves to 5, Chariot 3 moves to 5, General 5 moves to 6, Chariot 5 retreats 4, Soldier 4 advances 1, Chariot 5 moves to 6, Horse 6 advances to 4, General 6 advances 1, Soldier 3 advances 1, General 6 moves to 5, Soldier 3 advances 1, Pawn 7 moves to 6, Horse 9 retreats 7, Pawn 6 moves to 5, General 6 retreats 1, Pawn 4 moves to 3, Horse 3 retreats 5, Pawn 3 moves to 4, Horse 5 retreats 3, Pawn 5 moves to 6, General 6 advances 1, Pawn 4 moves to 3, Horse 3 advances to 5, Pawn 6 moves to 7, Horse 5 retreats 3.
